<pr_description>
Valid parameters for resource requests are rejected as "unknown flag"
### Issue
When using v1.28.0 of the CLI for various resource requests I'm getting various `unknown flag` errors for flags that are valid per documentation.

Example:
```
➜  ~ stripe tax_rates create  \
  --display-name=VAT \
  --description="VAT Germany" \
  --percentage=16 \
  --jurisdiction=DE \
  --inclusive=false
unknown flag: --percentage
```
Pulled directly from the CLI example here: https://docs.stripe.com/api/tax_rates/create?lang=cli

and

```
➜  ~ stripe coupons create  \
  --duration=repeating \
  --duration-in-months=3 \
  --percent-off=25.5
unknown flag: --percent-off
```
From: https://docs.stripe.com/api/coupons/create?lang=cli

This happens for additional resources, and it seems the commonality is that the parameter type is "float" in the docs, and in the `resource_cmds.go` file the flag type is specified as `"number"`. See: https://github.com/stripe/stripe-cli/blob/v1.28.0/pkg/cmd/resources_cmds.go#L958

### Expected Behavior
These flags/parameters should be valid in CLI usage.

### Steps to reproduce
This create command should work:
```
➜  ~ stripe coupons create  \
  --duration=repeating \
  --duration-in-months=3 \
  --percent-off=25.5
```

### Traceback
This was working in previous versions of the CLI, so I suspect that a relatively recent change did something to handling of these flags

### Environment
macOS


</pr_description>

    21	//
    22	// Public types
    23	//
    24	
    25	// OperationCmd represents operation commands. Operation commands are nested
    26	// under resource commands and represent a specific API operation for that
    27	// resource.
    28	//
    29	// Examples of operations: `create`, `retrieve` (standard CRUD methods),
    30	// `capture` (custom method for the `charges` resource).
    31	type OperationCmd struct {
    32	        *requests.Base
    33	
    34	        Name      string
    35	        HTTPVerb  string
    36	        Path      string
    37	        URLParams []string
    38	
    39	        IsPreviewCommand bool
    40	
    41	        stringFlags  map[string]*string
    42	        arrayFlags   map[string]*[]string
    43	        integerFlags map[string]*int
    44	        boolFlags    map[string]*bool
    45	}
    46	
    47	func (oc *OperationCmd) runOperationCmd(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {
    48	        if err := stripe.ValidateAPIBaseURL(oc.APIBaseURL); err != nil {
    49	                return err
    50	        }
    51	
    52	        apiKey, err := oc.Profile.GetAPIKey(oc.Livemode)
    53	        if err != nil {
    54	                return err
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        path := formatURL(oc.Path, args)
    58	        requestParams := make(map[string]interface{})
    59	        oc.addStringRequestParams(requestParams)
    60	        oc.addIntRequestParams(requestParams)
    61	        oc.addBoolRequestParams(requestParams)
    62	
    63	        err = oc.addArrayRequestParams(requestParams)
    64	        if err != nil {
    65	                return err
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        if oc.HTTPVerb == http.MethodDelete {
    69	                // display account information and confirm whether user wants to proceed
    70	                var mode = "Test"
    71	                displayName := oc.Profile.GetDisplayName()
    72	
    73	                if oc.Livemode {
    74	                        mode = "Live"
    75	                }
    76	
    77	                // display account information and confirmation to proceed
    78	                fmt.Printf("This command will be executed on the account with the following details:\n")
    79	                fmt.Printf("> Mode: %s\n", mode)
    80	                if displayName != "" {
    81	                        fmt.Printf("> Account Name: %s\n", displayName)
    82	                }
    83	                if strings.HasPrefix(path, "/v1/accounts/") {
    84	                        connectedAccountID := strings.Split(path, "/")[3]
    85	                        fmt.Printf("> Connected Account: %s\n", connectedAccountID)
    86	                }
    87	
    88	                // call the confirm command from base request
    89	                confirmation, err := oc.Confirm()
    90	                if err != nil {
    91	                        return err
    92	                } else if !confirmation {
    93	                        fmt.Println("Exiting without execution. User did not confirm the command.")
    94	                        return nil
    95	                }
    96	
    97	                // if confirmation is provided, make the request
    98	                _, err = oc.MakeRequest(cmd.Context(), apiKey, path, &oc.Parameters, requestParams, false, nil)
    99	
   100	                return err
   101	        }
   102	        // else
   103	        _, err = oc.MakeRequest(cmd.Context(), apiKey, path, &oc.Parameters, requestParams, false, nil)
   104	        return err
   105	}

   111	// NewUnsupportedV2BillingOperationCmd returns a new cobra command for an unsupported v2 billing command.
   112	// This is temporary until resource commands support the /v2/billing namespace.
   113	func NewUnsupportedV2BillingOperationCmd(parentCmd *cobra.Command, name string, path string) *cobra.Command {
   114	        cmd := &cobra.Command{
   115	                Use:         name,
   116	                Annotations: make(map[string]string),
   117	                Run: func(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) {
   118	                        output := `
   119	%s is not supported by Stripe CLI yet. Please use the %s or cURL to create a %s, instead.
   120	
   121	* Hint: If you're trying to test webhook events, you can always use %s or %s.
   122	                        `
   123	
   124	                        fmt.Println(fmt.Sprintf(output, ansi.Bold(path), ansi.Linkify("Dashboard", "https://dashboard.stripe.com", os.Stdout), parentCmd.Name(), ansi.Bold("stripe trigger v1.billing.meter.no_meter_found"), ansi.Bold("stripe trigger v1.billing.meter.error_report_triggered")))
   125	                },
   126	        }
   127	        parentCmd.AddCommand(cmd)
   128	        return cmd
   129	}
   130	
   131	// NewOperationCmd returns a new OperationCmd.
   132	func NewOperationCmd(parentCmd *cobra.Command, name, path, httpVerb string,
   133	        propFlags map[string]string, enumFlags map[string][]spec.StripeEnumValue, cfg *config.Config, isPreview bool) *OperationCmd {
   134	        urlParams := extractURLParams(path)
   135	        httpVerb = strings.ToUpper(httpVerb)
   136	        operationCmd := &OperationCmd{
   137	                Base: &requests.Base{
   138	                        Method:           httpVerb,
   139	                        Profile:          &cfg.Profile,
   140	                        IsPreviewCommand: isPreview,
   141	                },
   142	                Name:             name,
   143	                HTTPVerb:         httpVerb,
   144	                Path:             path,
   145	                URLParams:        urlParams,
   146	                IsPreviewCommand: isPreview,
   147	
   148	                arrayFlags:   make(map[string]*[]string),
   149	                stringFlags:  make(map[string]*string),
   150	                integerFlags: make(map[string]*int),
   151	                boolFlags:    make(map[string]*bool),
   152	        }
   153	        cmd := &cobra.Command{
   154	                Use:         name,
   155	                Annotations: make(map[string]string),
   156	                RunE:        operationCmd.runOperationCmd,
   157	                Args:        validators.ExactArgs(len(urlParams)),
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        for prop, propType := range propFlags {
   161	                // it's ok to treat all flags as string flags because we don't send any default flag values to the API
   162	                // i.e. "account_balance" default is "" not 0 but this is ok
   163	                flagName := strings.ReplaceAll(prop, "_", "-")
   164	
   165	                // Create flag description
   166	                var description string
   167	                if enums, hasEnum := enumFlags[prop]; hasEnum {
   168	                        // Create a description that includes enum values
   169	                        enumValues := []string{}
   170	                        for _, enum := range enums {
   171	                                enumValues = append(enumValues, fmt.Sprintf("%s (%s)", enum.Value, enum.Description))
   172	                        }
   173	                        description = fmt.Sprintf("Possible values: %s", strings.Join(enumValues, ", "))
   174	                } else {
   175	                        description = "" // Default empty description
   176	                }
   177	
   178	                switch propType {
   179	                case "array":
   180	                        operationCmd.arrayFlags[flagName] = cmd.Flags().StringArray(flagName, []string{}, description)
   181	                case "string":
   182	                        operationCmd.stringFlags[flagName] = cmd.Flags().String(flagName, "", description)
   183	                case "integer":
   184	                        operationCmd.integerFlags[flagName] = cmd.Flags().Int(flagName, -1, description)
   185	                case "boolean":
   186	                        operationCmd.boolFlags[flagName] = cmd.Flags().Bool(flagName, false, description)
   187	                default:
   188	                }
   189	                cmd.Flags().SetAnnotation(flagName, "request", []string{"true"})
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        cmd.SetUsageTemplate(operationUsageTemplate(urlParams))
   193	        cmd.DisableFlagsInUseLine = true
   194	        operationCmd.Cmd = cmd
   195	        operationCmd.InitFlags()
   196	
   197	        parentCmd.AddCommand(cmd)
   198	        parentCmd.Annotations[name] = "operation"
   199	
   200	        return operationCmd
   201	}
   202	
   203	//
   204	// Private functions
   205	//
   206	
   207	func extractURLParams(path string) []string {
   208	        re := regexp.MustCompile(`{\w+}`)
   209	        return re.FindAllString(path, -1)
   210	}
   211	
   212	func formatURL(path string, urlParams []string) string {
   213	        s := make([]interface{}, len(urlParams))
   214	        for i, v := range urlParams {
   215	                s[i] = v
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        re := regexp.MustCompile(`{\w+}`)
   219	        format := re.ReplaceAllString(path, "%s")
   220	
   221	        return fmt.Sprintf(format, s...)
   222	}
   223	
   224	func operationUsageTemplate(urlParams []string) string {
   225	        args := strings.Map(func(r rune) rune {
   226	                switch r {
   227	                case '{':
   228	                        return '<'
   229	                case '}':
   230	                        return '>'
   231	                }
   232	                return r
   233	        }, strings.Join(urlParams, " "))
   234	        if args != "" {
   235	                args += " "
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        args += "[--param=value] [-d \"nested[param]=value\"]"
   239	
   240	        return fmt.Sprintf(`%s{{if .Runnable}}
   241	  {{.UseLine}} %s{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableSubCommands}}
   242	  {{.CommandPath}} [command]{{end}}{{if gt (len .Aliases) 0}}
   243	
   244	%s
   245	  {{.NameAndAliases}}{{end}}{{if .HasExample}}
   246	
   247	%s
   248	{{.Example}}{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableSubCommands}}
   249	
   250	%s{{range .Commands}}{{if (or .IsAvailableCommand (eq .Name "help"))}}
   251	  {{rpad .Name .NamePadding }} {{.Short}}{{end}}{{end}}{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableLocalFlags}}
   252	
   253	%s
   254	{{WrappedRequestParamsFlagUsages . | trimTrailingWhitespaces}}
   255	
   256	%s
   257	
   258	%s
   259	{{WrappedNonRequestParamsFlagUsages . | trimTrailingWhitespaces}}{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableInheritedFlags}}
   260	
   261	%s
   262	{{WrappedInheritedFlagUsages . | trimTrailingWhitespaces}}{{end}}{{if .HasHelpSubCommands}}
   263	
   264	%s{{range .Commands}}{{if .IsAdditionalHelpTopicCommand}}
   265	  {{rpad .CommandPath .CommandPathPadding}} {{.Short}}{{end}}{{end}}{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableSubCommands}}
   266	
   267	Use "{{.CommandPath}} [command] --help" for more information about a command.{{end}}
   268	`,
   269	                ansi.Bold("Usage:"),
   270	                args,
   271	                ansi.Bold("Aliases:"),
   272	                ansi.Bold("Examples:"),
   273	                ansi.Bold("Available Operations:"),
   274	                ansi.Bold("Request Parameters:"),
   275	                ansi.Italic("Note: all types are specifically for the Stripe CLI itself, not the Stripe API. The CLI handles\ntransforming types to what the API expects."),
   276	                ansi.Bold("Flags:"),
   277	                ansi.Bold("Global Flags:"),
   278	                ansi.Bold("Additional help topics:"),
   279	        )
   280	}
   281	
   282	func constructParamFromDot(dotParam string) string {
   283	        paramPath := strings.Split(dotParam, ".")
   284	        var param string
   285	        for i, p := range paramPath {
   286	                if i == 0 {
   287	                        param = p
   288	                } else {
   289	                        param = fmt.Sprintf("%s[%s]", param, p)
   290	                }
   291	        }
   292	
   293	        return param
   294	}
   295	
   296	func (oc *OperationCmd) addStringRequestParams(requestParams map[string]interface{}) {
   297	        for stringProp, stringVal := range oc.stringFlags {
   298	                // only include fields explicitly set by the user to avoid conflicts between e.g. account_balance, balance
   299	                if oc.Cmd.Flags().Changed(stringProp) {
   300	                        paramName := getParamName(stringProp)
   301	                        if strings.Contains(paramName, ".") {
   302	                                constructedNestedStringParams(requestParams, strings.Split(paramName, "."), stringVal)
   303	                        } else {
   304	                                requestParams[paramName] = *stringVal
   305	                        }
   306	                }
   307	        }
   308	}
   309	
   310	func (oc *OperationCmd) addIntRequestParams(requestParams map[string]interface{}) {
   311	        for intProp, intVal := range oc.integerFlags {
   312	                if oc.Cmd.Flags().Changed(intProp) {
   313	                        paramName := getParamName(intProp)
   314	                        if strings.Contains(paramName, ".") {
   315	                                constructedNestedIntParams(requestParams, strings.Split(paramName, "."), intVal)
   316	                        } else {
   317	                                requestParams[paramName] = *intVal
   318	                        }
   319	                }
   320	        }
   321	}
   322	
   323	func (oc *OperationCmd) addBoolRequestParams(requestParams map[string]interface{}) {
   324	        for boolProp, boolVal := range oc.boolFlags {
   325	                if oc.Cmd.Flags().Changed(boolProp) {
   326	                        paramName := getParamName(boolProp)
   327	                        if strings.Contains(paramName, ".") {
   328	                                constructedNestedBoolParams(requestParams, strings.Split(paramName, "."), boolVal)
   329	                        } else {
   330	                                requestParams[paramName] = *boolVal
   331	                        }
   332	                }
   333	        }
   334	}
   335	
   336	func (oc *OperationCmd) addArrayRequestParams(requestParams map[string]interface{}) error {
   337	        for arrayProp, arrayVal := range oc.arrayFlags {
   338	                // only include fields explicitly set by the user to avoid conflicts between e.g. account_balance, balance
   339	                if oc.Cmd.Flags().Changed(arrayProp) {
   340	                        paramName := getParamName(arrayProp)
   341	                        for _, arrayItem := range *arrayVal {
   342	                                if strings.Contains(paramName, ".") {
   343	                                        constructedNestedArrayParams(requestParams, strings.Split(paramName, "."), arrayItem)
   344	                                } else {
   345	                                        if _, ok := requestParams[paramName]; !ok {
   346	                                                requestParams[paramName] = make([]interface{}, 0)
   347	                                        }
   348	                                        switch v := reflect.ValueOf(requestParams[paramName]); v.Kind() {
   349	                                        case reflect.Array, reflect.Slice:
   350	                                                requestParams[paramName] = append(requestParams[paramName].([]interface{}), arrayItem)
   351	                                        default:
   352	                                                return fmt.Errorf("array parameter flag %s has conflict with another non-array parameter flag", paramName)
   353	                                        }
   354	                                }
   355	                        }
   356	                }
   357	        }
   358	        return nil
   359	}
   360	
   361	func constructedNestedStringParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, stringVal *string) {
   362	        if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
   363	                return
   364	        }
   365	
   366	        field := paramKeys[0]
   367	
   368	        if len(paramKeys) == 1 {
   369	                params[field] = *stringVal
   370	                return
   371	        }
   372	
   373	        if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
   374	                params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
   375	        }
   376	
   377	        constructedNestedStringParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], stringVal)
   378	}
   379	
   380	func constructedNestedIntParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, intVal *int) {
   381	        if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
   382	                return
   383	        }
   384	
   385	        field := paramKeys[0]
   386	
   387	        if len(paramKeys) == 1 {
   388	                params[field] = *intVal
   389	                return
   390	        }
   391	
   392	        if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
   393	                params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
   394	        }
   395	
   396	        constructedNestedIntParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], intVal)
   397	}
   398	
   399	func constructedNestedBoolParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, boolVal *bool) {
   400	        if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
   401	                return
   402	        }
   403	
   404	        field := paramKeys[0]
   405	
   406	        if len(paramKeys) == 1 {
   407	                params[field] = *boolVal
   408	                return
   409	        }
   410	
   411	        if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
   412	                params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
   413	        }
   414	
   415	        constructedNestedBoolParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], boolVal)
   416	}
   417	
   418	func constructedNestedArrayParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, arrayVal string) {
   419	        if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
   420	                return
   421	        }
   422	
   423	        field := paramKeys[0]
   424	
   425	        if len(paramKeys) == 1 {
   426	                if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
   427	                        params[field] = make([]interface{}, 0)
   428	                }
   429	                params[field] = append(params[field].([]interface{}), arrayVal)
   430	                return
   431	        }
   432	
   433	        if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
   434	                params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
   435	        }
   436	
   437	        constructedNestedArrayParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], arrayVal)
   438	}
   439	
   440	func getParamName(prop string) string {
   441	        return strings.ReplaceAll(prop, "-", "_")
   442	}

type OperationCmd struct {
	*requests.Base

	Name      string
	HTTPVerb  string
	Path      string
	URLParams []string

	IsPreviewCommand bool

	stringFlags  map[string]*string
	arrayFlags   map[string]*[]string
	integerFlags map[string]*int
	boolFlags    map[string]*bool
}

func (oc *OperationCmd) runOperationCmd(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {
	if err := stripe.ValidateAPIBaseURL(oc.APIBaseURL); err != nil {
		return err
	}

	apiKey, err := oc.Profile.GetAPIKey(oc.Livemode)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	path := formatURL(oc.Path, args)
	requestParams := make(map[string]interface{})
	oc.addStringRequestParams(requestParams)
	oc.addIntRequestParams(requestParams)

package resource

import (
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"reflect"
	"regexp"
	"strings"

	"github.com/spf13/cobra"

	"github.com/stripe/stripe-cli/pkg/ansi"
	"github.com/stripe/stripe-cli/pkg/config"
	"github.com/stripe/stripe-cli/pkg/requests"

	"github.com/stripe/stripe-cli/pkg/stripe"
	"github.com/stripe/stripe-cli/pkg/validators"

//
// Public types
//

// OperationCmd represents operation commands. Operation commands are nested
// under resource commands and represent a specific API operation for that
// resource.
//
// Examples of operations: `create`, `retrieve` (standard CRUD methods),
// `capture` (custom method for the `charges` resource).
type OperationCmd struct {
	*requests.Base

	Name      string
	HTTPVerb  string
	Path      string
	URLParams []string

	IsPreviewCommand bool

	stringFlags  map[string]*string
	arrayFlags   map[string]*[]string
	integerFlags map[string]*int
	boolFlags    map[string]*bool
}

func (oc *OperationCmd) runOperationCmd(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {
	if err := stripe.ValidateAPIBaseURL(oc.APIBaseURL); err != nil {
		return err
	}

	apiKey, err := oc.Profile.GetAPIKey(oc.Livemode)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	path := formatURL(oc.Path, args)
	requestParams := make(map[string]interface{})
	oc.addStringRequestParams(requestParams)
	oc.addIntRequestParams(requestParams)
	oc.addBoolRequestParams(requestParams)

	err = oc.addArrayRequestParams(requestParams)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	if oc.HTTPVerb == http.MethodDelete {
		// display account information and confirm whether user wants to proceed
		var mode = "Test"
		displayName := oc.Profile.GetDisplayName()

		if oc.Livemode {
			mode = "Live"
		}

		// display account information and confirmation to proceed
		fmt.Printf("This command will be executed on the account with the following details:\n")
		fmt.Printf("> Mode: %s\n", mode)
		if displayName != "" {
			fmt.Printf("> Account Name: %s\n", displayName)
		}
		if strings.HasPrefix(path, "/v1/accounts/") {
			connectedAccountID := strings.Split(path, "/")[3]
			fmt.Printf("> Connected Account: %s\n", connectedAccountID)
		}

		// call the confirm command from base request
		confirmation, err := oc.Confirm()
		if err != nil {
			return err
		} else if !confirmation {
			fmt.Println("Exiting without execution. User did not confirm the command.")
			return nil
		}

		// if confirmation is provided, make the request
		_, err = oc.MakeRequest(cmd.Context(), apiKey, path, &oc.Parameters, requestParams, false, nil)

		return err
	}
	// else
	_, err = oc.MakeRequest(cmd.Context(), apiKey, path, &oc.Parameters, requestParams, false, nil)
	return err
}

//
// Public functions
//

// NewUnsupportedV2BillingOperationCmd returns a new cobra command for an unsupported v2 billing command.
// This is temporary until resource commands support the /v2/billing namespace.
func NewUnsupportedV2BillingOperationCmd(parentCmd *cobra.Command, name string, path string) *cobra.Command {
	cmd := &cobra.Command{
		Use:         name,
		Annotations: make(map[string]string),
		Run: func(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) {
			output := `
%s is not supported by Stripe CLI yet. Please use the %s or cURL to create a %s, instead.

* Hint: If you're trying to test webhook events, you can always use %s or %s.
			`

			fmt.Println(fmt.Sprintf(output, ansi.Bold(path), ansi.Linkify("Dashboard", "https://dashboard.stripe.com", os.Stdout), parentCmd.Name(), ansi.Bold("stripe trigger v1.billing.meter.no_meter_found"), ansi.Bold("stripe trigger v1.billing.meter.error_report_triggered")))
		},
	}
	parentCmd.AddCommand(cmd)
	return cmd
}

// NewOperationCmd returns a new OperationCmd.
func NewOperationCmd(parentCmd *cobra.Command, name, path, httpVerb string,
	propFlags map[string]string, enumFlags map[string][]spec.StripeEnumValue, cfg *config.Config, isPreview bool) *OperationCmd {
	urlParams := extractURLParams(path)
	httpVerb = strings.ToUpper(httpVerb)
	operationCmd := &OperationCmd{
		Base: &requests.Base{
			Method:           httpVerb,
			Profile:          &cfg.Profile,
			IsPreviewCommand: isPreview,
		},
		Name:             name,
		HTTPVerb:         httpVerb,
		Path:             path,
		URLParams:        urlParams,
		IsPreviewCommand: isPreview,

		arrayFlags:   make(map[string]*[]string),
		stringFlags:  make(map[string]*string),
		integerFlags: make(map[string]*int),
		boolFlags:    make(map[string]*bool),
	}
	cmd := &cobra.Command{
		Use:         name,
		Annotations: make(map[string]string),
		RunE:        operationCmd.runOperationCmd,
		Args:        validators.ExactArgs(len(urlParams)),
	}

	for prop, propType := range propFlags {
		// it's ok to treat all flags as string flags because we don't send any default flag values to the API
		// i.e. "account_balance" default is "" not 0 but this is ok
		flagName := strings.ReplaceAll(prop, "_", "-")

		// Create flag description
		var description string
		if enums, hasEnum := enumFlags[prop]; hasEnum {
			// Create a description that includes enum values
			enumValues := []string{}
			for _, enum := range enums {
				enumValues = append(enumValues, fmt.Sprintf("%s (%s)", enum.Value, enum.Description))
			}
			description = fmt.Sprintf("Possible values: %s", strings.Join(enumValues, ", "))
		} else {
			description = "" // Default empty description
		}

		switch propType {
		case "array":
			operationCmd.arrayFlags[flagName] = cmd.Flags().StringArray(flagName, []string{}, description)
		case "string":
			operationCmd.stringFlags[flagName] = cmd.Flags().String(flagName, "", description)
		case "integer":
			operationCmd.integerFlags[flagName] = cmd.Flags().Int(flagName, -1, description)
		case "boolean":
			operationCmd.boolFlags[flagName] = cmd.Flags().Bool(flagName, false, description)
		default:
		}
		cmd.Flags().SetAnnotation(flagName, "request", []string{"true"})
	}

	cmd.SetUsageTemplate(operationUsageTemplate(urlParams))
	cmd.DisableFlagsInUseLine = true
	operationCmd.Cmd = cmd
	operationCmd.InitFlags()

	parentCmd.AddCommand(cmd)
	parentCmd.Annotations[name] = "operation"

	return operationCmd
}

//
// Private functions
//

func extractURLParams(path string) []string {
	re := regexp.MustCompile(`{\w+}`)
	return re.FindAllString(path, -1)
}

func formatURL(path string, urlParams []string) string {
	s := make([]interface{}, len(urlParams))
	for i, v := range urlParams {
		s[i] = v
	}

	re := regexp.MustCompile(`{\w+}`)
	format := re.ReplaceAllString(path, "%s")

	return fmt.Sprintf(format, s...)
}

func operationUsageTemplate(urlParams []string) string {
	args := strings.Map(func(r rune) rune {
		switch r {
		case '{':
			return '<'
		case '}':
			return '>'
		}
		return r
	}, strings.Join(urlParams, " "))
	if args != "" {
		args += " "
	}

	args += "[--param=value] [-d \"nested[param]=value\"]"

	return fmt.Sprintf(`%s{{if .Runnable}}
  {{.UseLine}} %s{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableSubCommands}}
  {{.CommandPath}} [command]{{end}}{{if gt (len .Aliases) 0}}

%s
  {{.NameAndAliases}}{{end}}{{if .HasExample}}

%s
{{.Example}}{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableSubCommands}}

%s{{range .Commands}}{{if (or .IsAvailableCommand (eq .Name "help"))}}
  {{rpad .Name .NamePadding }} {{.Short}}{{end}}{{end}}{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableLocalFlags}}

%s
{{WrappedRequestParamsFlagUsages . | trimTrailingWhitespaces}}

%s

%s
{{WrappedNonRequestParamsFlagUsages . | trimTrailingWhitespaces}}{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableInheritedFlags}}

%s
{{WrappedInheritedFlagUsages . | trimTrailingWhitespaces}}{{end}}{{if .HasHelpSubCommands}}

%s{{range .Commands}}{{if .IsAdditionalHelpTopicCommand}}
  {{rpad .CommandPath .CommandPathPadding}} {{.Short}}{{end}}{{end}}{{end}}{{if .HasAvailableSubCommands}}

Use "{{.CommandPath}} [command] --help" for more information about a command.{{end}}
`,
		ansi.Bold("Usage:"),
		args,
		ansi.Bold("Aliases:"),
		ansi.Bold("Examples:"),
		ansi.Bold("Available Operations:"),
		ansi.Bold("Request Parameters:"),
		ansi.Italic("Note: all types are specifically for the Stripe CLI itself, not the Stripe API. The CLI handles\ntransforming types to what the API expects."),
		ansi.Bold("Flags:"),
		ansi.Bold("Global Flags:"),
		ansi.Bold("Additional help topics:"),
	)
}

func constructParamFromDot(dotParam string) string {
	paramPath := strings.Split(dotParam, ".")
	var param string
	for i, p := range paramPath {
		if i == 0 {
			param = p
		} else {
			param = fmt.Sprintf("%s[%s]", param, p)
		}
	}

	return param
}

func (oc *OperationCmd) addStringRequestParams(requestParams map[string]interface{}) {
	for stringProp, stringVal := range oc.stringFlags {
		// only include fields explicitly set by the user to avoid conflicts between e.g. account_balance, balance
		if oc.Cmd.Flags().Changed(stringProp) {
			paramName := getParamName(stringProp)
			if strings.Contains(paramName, ".") {
				constructedNestedStringParams(requestParams, strings.Split(paramName, "."), stringVal)
			} else {
				requestParams[paramName] = *stringVal
			}
		}
	}
}

func (oc *OperationCmd) addIntRequestParams(requestParams map[string]interface{}) {
	for intProp, intVal := range oc.integerFlags {
		if oc.Cmd.Flags().Changed(intProp) {
			paramName := getParamName(intProp)
			if strings.Contains(paramName, ".") {
				constructedNestedIntParams(requestParams, strings.Split(paramName, "."), intVal)
			} else {
				requestParams[paramName] = *intVal
			}
		}
	}
}

func (oc *OperationCmd) addBoolRequestParams(requestParams map[string]interface{}) {
	for boolProp, boolVal := range oc.boolFlags {
		if oc.Cmd.Flags().Changed(boolProp) {
			paramName := getParamName(boolProp)
			if strings.Contains(paramName, ".") {
				constructedNestedBoolParams(requestParams, strings.Split(paramName, "."), boolVal)
			} else {
				requestParams[paramName] = *boolVal
			}
		}
	}
}

func (oc *OperationCmd) addArrayRequestParams(requestParams map[string]interface{}) error {
	for arrayProp, arrayVal := range oc.arrayFlags {
		// only include fields explicitly set by the user to avoid conflicts between e.g. account_balance, balance
		if oc.Cmd.Flags().Changed(arrayProp) {
			paramName := getParamName(arrayProp)
			for _, arrayItem := range *arrayVal {
				if strings.Contains(paramName, ".") {
					constructedNestedArrayParams(requestParams, strings.Split(paramName, "."), arrayItem)
				} else {
					if _, ok := requestParams[paramName]; !ok {
						requestParams[paramName] = make([]interface{}, 0)
					}
					switch v := reflect.ValueOf(requestParams[paramName]); v.Kind() {
					case reflect.Array, reflect.Slice:
						requestParams[paramName] = append(requestParams[paramName].([]interface{}), arrayItem)
					default:
						return fmt.Errorf("array parameter flag %s has conflict with another non-array parameter flag", paramName)
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	return nil
}

func constructedNestedStringParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, stringVal *string) {
	if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
		return
	}

	field := paramKeys[0]

	if len(paramKeys) == 1 {
		params[field] = *stringVal
		return
	}

	if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
		params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
	}

	constructedNestedStringParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], stringVal)
}

func constructedNestedIntParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, intVal *int) {
	if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
		return
	}

	field := paramKeys[0]

	if len(paramKeys) == 1 {
		params[field] = *intVal
		return
	}

	if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
		params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
	}

	constructedNestedIntParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], intVal)
}

func constructedNestedBoolParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, boolVal *bool) {
	if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
		return
	}

	field := paramKeys[0]

	if len(paramKeys) == 1 {
		params[field] = *boolVal
		return
	}

	if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
		params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
	}

	constructedNestedBoolParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], boolVal)
}

func constructedNestedArrayParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, arrayVal string) {
	if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
		return
	}

	field := paramKeys[0]

	if len(paramKeys) == 1 {
		if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
			params[field] = make([]interface{}, 0)
		}
		params[field] = append(params[field].([]interface{}), arrayVal)
		return
	}

	if _, ok := params[field]; !ok {
		params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
	}

	constructedNestedArrayParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], arrayVal)
}

func getParamName(prop string) string {
	return strings.ReplaceAll(prop, "-", "_")
}

+func constructedNestedFloatParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, floatVal *float64) {
+	if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
+		return
+	}

+func constructedNestedFloatParams(params map[string]interface{}, paramKeys []string, floatVal *float64) {
+	if len(paramKeys) == 0 {
+		return
+	}
+
+	field := paramKeys[0]
+

+		params[field] = *floatVal
+		return
+	}

+		params[field] = make(map[string]interface{}, 0)
+	}
+
+	constructedNestedFloatParams(params[field].(map[string]interface{}), paramKeys[1:], floatVal)
+}

+import os
+import subprocess
+
+def test_stripe_coupons_create():
+    cmd = [
+        "go", "run", "cmd/stripe/main.go", "coupons", "create",
+        "--duration=repeating",
+        "--duration-in-months=3",
+        "--percent-off=25.5"
+    ]
+    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, cwd="/testbed")
+    print(f"STDOUT: {result.stdout}")
+    print(f"STDERR: {result.stderr}")
+    if "unknown flag: --percent-off" in result.stderr:
+        print("Successfully reproduced 'unknown flag: --percent-off'")
+    else:
+        print("Failed to reproduce 'unknown flag: --percent-off'")
+
